```yaml
          - link "Your Ads Privacy Choices" [ref=e3853] [cursor=pointer]:
            - /url: /privacyprefs?ref_=footer_iba
        - listitem [ref=e3854]
      - generic [ref=e3856]: © 1996-2026, Amazon.com, Inc. or its affiliates
```
